    "code": 'import requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport json\nimport re\nimport time\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# Create workspace directory if it doesn\'t exist\nimport os\nif not os.path.exists(\'workspace\'):\n    os.makedirs(\'workspace\')\n\nprint("=== MICHAEL JACKSON DISCOGRAPHY RESEARCH ===\\n")\nprint("Objective: Identify the King of Pop\'s sixth studio album and its fifth single\\n")\n\n# Set up headers for web requests\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36\'\n}\n\n# Target URLs for Michael Jackson discography research\ntarget_urls = {\n    \'mj_main\': "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Jackson",\n    \'mj_discography\': "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Jackson_discography",\n    \'mj_solo_discography\': "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Jackson_solo_discography"\n}\n\nsuccessful_sources = []\nfailed_sources = []\n\nprint("=== PHASE 1: ACCESSING MICHAEL JACKSON WIKIPEDIA PAGES ===\\n")\n\n# Process each URL\nfor source_name, url in target_urls.items():\n    print(f"--- Accessing {source_name} ---")\n    print(f"URL: {url}")\n    \n    try:\n        response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=20)\n        print(f"Response status: {response.status_code}")\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            print(f"✓ Successfully accessed {url}")\n            \n            # Save the content for analysis\n            filename = source_name + \'.html\'\n            filepath = f\'workspace/{filename}\'\n            \n            with open(filepath, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                f.write(response.text)\n            \n            # Quick content analysis\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            title = soup.find(\'title\')\n            title_text = title.get_text().strip() if title else \'No title found\'\n            \n            # Look for discography/album related content\n            content_text = soup.get_text().lower()\n            discography_indicators = [\n                \'discography\', \'album\', \'studio album\', \'single\', \'thriller\', \'bad\', \'dangerous\',\n                \'history\', \'invincible\', \'off the wall\', \'solo career\', \'king of pop\'\n            ]\n            has_discography_info = any(indicator in content_text for indicator in discography_indicators)\n            \n            # Look for specific album titles that might be his sixth\n            known_albums = [\n                \'off the wall\', \'thriller\', \'bad\', \'dangerous\', \'history\', \'invincible\',\n                \'blood on the dance floor\', \'xscape\', \'michael\'\n            ]\n            \n            album_mentions = []\n            for album_hint in known_albums:\n                if album_hint in content_text:\n                    album_mentions.append(album_hint)\n            \n            successful_sources.append({\n                \'source_name\': source_name,\n                \'url\': url,\n                \'title\': title_text,\n                \'filename\': filepath,\n                \'has_discography_info\': has_discography_info,\n                \'content_length\': len(response.text),\n                \'album_mentions\': album_mentions\n            })\n            \n            print(f"  Title: {title_text}")\n            print(f"  Content length: {len(response.text)} characters")\n            print(f"  Contains discography info: {has_discography_info}")\n            print(f"  Album mentions found: {album_mentions}")\n            \n        else:\n            failed_sources.append({\'source_name\': source_name, \'url\': url, \'status\': response.status_code})\n            print(f"✗ Failed to access {url} - Status: {response.status_code}")\n            \n    except Exception as e:\n        failed_sources.append({\'source_name\': source_name, \'url\': url, \'error\': str(e)})\n        print(f"✗ Error accessing {url}: {str(e)}")\n    \n    print()\n    time.sleep(2)  # Be respectful to servers\n\nprint(f"=== INITIAL ACCESS RESULTS ===\\n")\nprint(f"Successfully accessed: {len(successful_sources)} sources")\nprint(f"Failed to access: {len(failed_sources)} sources")\n\n# Analyze successful sources for discography content\nif successful_sources:\n    print("\\n=== ANALYZING SUCCESSFUL SOURCES ===\\n")\n    \n    for i, source in enumerate(successful_sources, 1):\n        print(f"{i}. {source[\'source_name\']}")\n        print(f"   URL: {source[\'url\']}")\n        print(f"   Title: {source[\'title\']}")\n        print(f"   File saved: {source[\'filename\']}")\n        print(f"   Has discography info: {source[\'has_discography_info\']}")\n        print(f"   Album mentions: {source[\'album_mentions\']}")\n        \n        if source[\'has_discography_info\']:\n            print(f"   *** PRIORITY SOURCE - Contains discography information ***")\n        print()\n    \n    # Detailed analysis of priority sources\n    priority_sources = [s for s in successful_sources if s[\'has_discography_info\']]\n    \n    if priority_sources:\n        print(f"=== DETAILED DISCOGRAPHY ANALYSIS ===\\n")\n        print(f"Found {len(priority_sources)} priority sources with discography information\\n")\n        \n        mj_analysis = {}\n        \n        for source in priority_sources:\n            source_name = source[\'source_name\']\n            print(f"--- Analyzing {source_name} ---")\n            \n            with open(source[\'filename\'], \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                html_content = f.read()\n            \n            soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Look for discography section\n            discography_sections = []\n            headings = soup.find_all([\'h1\', \'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\', \'h5\', \'h6\'])\n            for heading in headings:\n                heading_text = heading.get_text().lower()\n                if any(word in heading_text for word in [\'discography\', \'albums\', \'studio albums\', \'solo career\', \'career\']):\n                    discography_sections.append({\n                        \'heading\': heading.get_text().strip(),\n                        \'level\': heading.name,\n                        \'element\': heading\n                    })\n            \n            print(f"Found {len(discography_sections)} discography-related sections:")\n            for section in discography_sections:\n                print(f"  - {section[\'level\'].upper()}: {section[\'heading\']}")\n            \n            # Look for tables that might contain album information\n            tables = soup.find_all(\'table\')\n            print(f"Found {len(tables)} tables in the page")\n            \n            # Analyze tables for album data\n            album_tables = []\n            for i, table in enumerate(tables):\n                table_text = table.get_text().lower()\n                \n                # Check if table contains album/year information\n                has_album_indicators = any(word in table_text for word in [\'album\', \'title\', \'year\', \'studio\', \'release\', \'single\'])\n                has_mj_albums = any(album in table_text for album in [\'thriller\', \'bad\', \'dangerous\', \'history\', \'invincible\', \'off the wall\'])\n                \n                if has_album_indicators and has_mj_albums:\n                    album_tables.append({\n                        \'index\': i,\n                        \'element\': table,\n                        \'has_mj_albums\': has_mj_albums\n                    })\n                    print(f"  Table {i+1}: Contains MJ album data - *** POTENTIAL DISCOGRAPHY TABLE ***")\n                elif has_album_indicators:\n                    print(f"  Table {i+1}: Contains general album data")\n                else:\n                    print(f"  Table {i+1}: General content")\n            \n            # Look for years in MJ\'s career range\n            career_year_pattern = r\'19[7-9][0-9]|20[0-2][0-9]\'\n            years_found = re.findall(career_year_pattern, soup.get_text())\n            unique_years = sorted(set(years_found))\n            \n            print(f"Years in MJ career range found: {unique_years[:20]}...")  # Show first 20\n            \n            # Look for specific album titles and order indicators\n            album_keywords = [\'debut album\', \'studio album\', \'first album\', \'second album\', \'third album\', \'fourth album\', \'fifth album\', \'sixth album\']\n            album_order_mentions = []\n            \n            for keyword in album_keywords:\n                if keyword in soup.get_text().lower():\n                    album_order_mentions.append(keyword)\n            \n            print(f"Album order keywords found: {album_order_mentions}")\n            \n            # Store analysis for this source\n            mj_analysis[source_name] = {\n                \'source_url\': source[\'url\'],\n                \'discography_sections_found\': len(discography_sections),\n                \'album_tables_identified\': len(album_tables),\n                \'career_years_found\': len(unique_years),\n                \'album_order_keywords\': album_order_mentions,\n                \'content_indicators\': {\n                    \'has_discography_section\': len(discography_sections) > 0,\n                    \'has_album_tables\': len(album_tables) > 0,\n                    \'has_career_years\': len(unique_years) > 0\n                }\n            }\n            \n            print()\n        \n        # Save comprehensive analysis\n        comprehensive_analysis = {\n            \'research_target\': \'Michael Jackson sixth studio album and fifth single\',\n            \'analysis_timestamp\': datetime.now().strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\'),\n            \'sources_analyzed\': list(mj_analysis.keys()),\n            \'total_priority_sources\': len(priority_sources),\n            \'mj_analysis\': mj_analysis\n        }\n        \n        with open(\'workspace/michael_jackson_preliminary_analysis.json\', \'w\') as f:\n            json.dump(comprehensive_analysis, f, indent=2)\n        \n        print(f"Comprehensive analysis saved to: workspace/michael_jackson_preliminary_analysis.json")\n        \n    else:\n        print("\\nNo sources with discography information found.")\nelse:\n    print("\\nNo sources successfully accessed.     "code": 'import os\nimport json\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport re\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nprint("=== MICHAEL JACKSON DISCOGRAPHY PARSING - PHASE 2 ===\\n")\nprint("Objective: Parse HTML content to identify sixth studio album and its fifth single\\n")\n\n# First, let\'s inspect the workspace to understand what files we have\nprint("=== WORKSPACE INSPECTION ===\\n")\n\nif os.path.exists(\'workspace\'):\n    workspace_files = os.listdir(\'workspace\')\n    print(f"Files in workspace: {len(workspace_files)}")\n    \n    for file in workspace_files:\n        file_path = os.path.join(\'workspace\', file)\n        file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)\n        print(f"  - {file} ({file_size:,} bytes)")\n        \n        # If it\'s a JSON file, let\'s peek at its structure\n        if file.endswith(\'.json\'):\n            print(f"    Inspecting JSON structure of {file}:")\n            with open(file_path, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                json_data = json.load(f)\n            \n            if isinstance(json_data, dict):\n                print(f"      Top-level keys: {list(json_data.keys())}")\n                for key, value in json_data.items():\n                    if isinstance(value, (list, dict)):\n                        print(f"        {key}: {type(value).__name__} with {len(value)} items")\n                    else:\n                        print(f"        {key}: {type(value).__name__} = {str(value)[:100]}...")\n            print()\nelse:\n    print("No workspace directory found")\n\n# Load the HTML files and start parsing for Michael Jackson\'s studio albums\nhtml_files = [f for f in os.listdir(\'workspace\') if f.endswith(\'.html\')]\nprint(f"\\n=== PARSING {len(html_files)} HTML FILES FOR STUDIO ALBUM CHRONOLOGY ===\\n")\n\n# Initialize results structure\nmj_discography = {\n    \'artist_name\': \'Michael Jackson\',\n    \'studio_albums\': [],\n    \'sources_parsed\': [],\n    \'analysis_notes\': []\n}\n\n# Parse each HTML file\nfor html_file in html_files:\n    print(f"--- Parsing {html_file} ---")\n    \n    filepath = f"workspace/{html_file}"\n    with open(filepath, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        html_content = f.read()\n    \n    soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, \'html.parser\')\n    \n    # Extract page title for verification\n    page_title = soup.find(\'title\')\n    title_text = page_title.get_text().strip() if page_title else \'No title\'\n    print(f"  Page title: {title_text}")\n    \n    # Record source\n    mj_discography[\'sources_parsed\'].append({\n        \'filename\': html_file,\n        \'title\': title_text,\n        \'file_size\': len(html_content)\n    })\n    \n    # Look for studio albums section specifically\n    print(f"  Searching for studio albums section...")\n    \n    # Find studio albums heading\n    headings = soup.find_all([\'h1\', \'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\', \'h5\', \'h6\'])\n    studio_albums_headings = []\n    \n    for heading in headings:\n        heading_text = heading.get_text().lower()\n        if \'studio album\' in heading_text or (heading_text == \'discography\' and \'discography\' in html_file):\n            studio_albums_headings.append({\n                \'text\': heading.get_text().strip(),\n                \'level\': heading.name,\n                \'element\': heading\n            })\n    \n    print(f"  Found {len(studio_albums_headings)} studio albums headings:")\n    for heading in studio_albums_headings:\n        print(f"    - {heading[\'level\'].upper()}: {heading[\'text\']}")\n    \n    # Look for tables with studio album information\n    tables = soup.find_all(\'table\')\n    print(f"  Found {len(tables)} tables")\n    \n    studio_album_tables = []\n    \n    for i, table in enumerate(tables):\n        table_text = table.get_text()\n        \n        # Check for studio album indicators\n        studio_indicators = [\'studio album\', \'album title\', \'release date\', \'year\']\n        has_studio_indicators = any(indicator.lower() in table_text.lower() for indicator in studio_indicators)\n        \n        # Check for known MJ studio albums\n        known_studio_albums = [\'off the wall\', \'thriller\', \'bad\', \'dangerous\', \'history\', \'invincible\']\n        has_mj_studio_albums = any(album in table_text.lower() for album in known_studio_albums)\n        \n        if has_studio_indicators and has_mj_studio_albums:\n            studio_album_tables.append({\n                \'index\': i,\n                \'table\': table\n            })\n            print(f"    Table {i+1}: *** STUDIO ALBUM TABLE - Contains MJ studio albums ***")\n        elif has_studio_indicators:\n            print(f"    Table {i+1}: Contains album data (general)")\n        else:\n            print(f"    Table {i+1}: Other content")\n    \n    print(f"  Identified {len(studio_album_tables)} studio album tables")\n    \n    # Extract studio album information from tables\n    for table_info in studio_album_tables:\n        table = table_info[\'table\']\n        print(f"\\n    Extracting from Studio Album Table {table_info[\'index\']+1}:")\n        \n        # Get table headers\n        headers = table.find_all(\'th\')\n        header_texts = [th.get_text().strip() for th in headers]\n        print(f"      Headers: {header_texts}")\n        \n        # Get table rows\n        rows = table.find_all(\'tr\')\n        \n        for row_idx, row in enumerate(rows[1:], 1):  # Skip header row\n            cells = row.find_all([\'td\', \'th\'])\n            if len(cells) >= 2:  # Need at least 2 columns\n                cell_texts = [cell.get_text().strip() for cell in cells]\n                row_text = \' \'.join(cell_texts)\n                \n                # Look for known studio albums\n                studio_album_found = None\n                for album in known_studio_albums:\n                    if album in row_text.lower():\n                        studio_album_found = album\n                        break\n                \n                if studio_album_found:\n                    print(f"        Row {row_idx}: {cell_texts}")\n                    \n                    # Extract year\n                    years_in_row = re.findall(r\'19[7-9][0-9]|20[0-2][0-9]\', row_text)\n                    \n                    # Try to identify album title more precisely\n                    album_title = None\n                    for cell in cell_texts:\n                        if studio_album_found.replace(\' \', \'\').lower() in cell.replace(\' \', \'\').lower():\n                            album_title = cell\n                            break\n                    \n                    if not album_title:\n                        album_title = studio_album_found.title()\n                    \n                    # Search for Invincible-related content\n        page_text = soup.get_text().lower()\n        \n        if \'invincible\' in page_text:\n            print(f"  Found \'Invincible\' mentions in {html_file}")\n            \n            # Look for singles information in tables\n            tables = soup.find_all(\'table\')\n            print(f"  Analyzing {len(tables)} tables for singles data...")\n            \n            for i, table in enumerate(tables):\n                table_text = table.get_text().lower()\n                \n                # Check if table contains Invincible and singles information\n                if \'invincible\' in table_text and (\'single\' in table_text or \'chart\' in table_text):\n                    print(f"    Table {i+1}: Contains Invincible singles data")\n                    \n                    # Get table rows\n                    rows = table.find_all(\'tr\')\n                    \n                    for row_idx, row in enumerate(rows):\n                        cells = row.find_all([\'td\', \'th\'])\n                        if len(cells) >= 2:\n                            cell_texts = [cell.get_text().strip() for cell in cells]\n                            row_text = \' \'.join(cell_texts).lower()\n                            \n                            # Look for potential singles from Invincible\n                            if \'invincible\' in row_text or any(year in row_text for year in [\'2001\', \'2002\', \'2003\']):\n                                # Try to extract release information\n                                        years_found = re.findall(r\'200[0-9]\', \' \'.join(cell_texts))\n                                        \n                                        single_info = {\n                                            \'title\': single.title(),\n                                            \'raw_data\': cell_texts,\n                                            \'years_found\': years_found,\n                                            \'source_table\': i + 1,\n                                            \'source_row\': row_idx + 1,\n                                            \'source_file\': html_file\n                                        }\n                                        \n                                        # Check if we already have this single\n                                        existing = None\n                                        for existing_single in invincible_singles:\n                                            if existing_single[\'title\'].lower() == single:\n                                                existing = existing_single\n                                                break\n                                        \n                                        if not existing:\n                                            invincible_singles.append(single_info)\n                                            print(f"        → Added: {single_info[\'title\']}")\n\n# If we didn\'t find enough singles info from HTML parsing, let\'s use known information\nif len(invincible_singles) < 5:\n    print("\\n=== USING KNOWN INVINCIBLE SINGLES INFORMATION ===\\n")\n    print("Based on music industry records, the singles from Invincible album were:")\n    \n    #
